【NO EOD FILES】
问题: NO EOD FILES

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Deadlock or SQL Timeout

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

Affected Stores:
0139 SVI BAG
0726 SVI NAGA
2278 SVI PRTO
5719 SVI CAL

Upon checking by POS Support in DMALL OS In-Store POS Server Reconciliation Mgt , "No da

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:In-store POS Server Reconciliation Managementpage shows“No Data is Found”
Root Cause Analysis:The reconciliation task for the affected stores failed due to a MySQL connection failure on DMall’s end.
Since store reconciliation is processed sequentially (e.g., Store A → Store B → Store C), the failure occurred when the system was reconciling the affected stores, at which point the MySQL connection on DMall’s end timed out.
Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.Informed Maam Chanda about the investigation findings,root cause, temporary and long-term solutions.
3. Asked approval to manually retry the reconciliation task/process for the affected store and generate the EOD files.
4.R&D team manually re-run the reconciliation task/process for the affected stores TD: December 19, 2025.
5.As confirmed by Ms. Catlin,the EOD files are now complete and available in their respective SFTP folders.Resolved the ticket.

【MOST OF THE POS ENCOUNTERED ERRORS】
问题: MOST OF THE POS ENCOUNTERED ERRORS

根因分类: Network / Connectivity Failure

具体根因: Network - ISP Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request: QR Code generation for promotion
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue:
MOST OF THE POS ENCOUNTERED ERRORS AFTER THE PRE-COMMIT PROCESS, RESULTING IN CASHIERS BEING OVER OR SHORT BY LARGE AMOUNTS OF MONEY.

解决摘要: --

解决方案:
Define Issue:POS pre-commit data is not accurate

Root Cause Analysis:POS connection issue / Offline ISP
POS can't connect to the ISP and Cloud during shift handover; uses the POS local data.

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket.
2.Based on the logs and continuous ping, the POScan't connect to the ISP and the Cloud during shift handover therefore the system utilized the POS local data for the pre-commit records.
3. Also based on the monitoring tool, the ISP of SVI BF Parañaquewas offline during and after the pre-commit.4. Informed the store that the pre-commit data may not be fully accurate; however, the POS Real-time Sales and Term-Z net amounts remain balanced. Therefore, no discrepancies are expected during the Accounting audit. This behavior is considered normal under such circumstances.
5.Resolved the ticket.

【Missing Roving POS EJ】
问题: Missing Roving POS EJ

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Application Issue

问题描述: Missing consolidated EJ of SVI Baguio at SFTP dated May 22, 2025. No findings on DMALL EJ audit tool.

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:DMall Bug/The reconciliation logic still usesMySQL, since reconciliation is donedaily. However, because ofdata archiving, MySQL only keepsone month of data, so it cannot find the data fromMay last year, which causes the reconciliation to get stuck and theConsolidated EJ is not generated.
Problem # 320
Related to ticket#6377512

Issue Description:Missing Roving POS EJ


Troubleshooting process:
1.Acknowledge the ticket.
2.An online order was picked up across different POS machines. During this process when the POS was in the online order page, the POS restarted. After the restart, the recovery mechanism pushed this online order to the cloudeven though payment was not completed, so it should not have been pushed (DMall Bug).
3. This isProblem 170, which was released to production on2025-09-17(version202509_4_PRODFIX_POS).4. However, the order happened inMay, before the fix was applied, so it was not covered.
5. This issue causedone extra receiptto be generated. The original order and receipt data themselves are correct.
6. Our Team already deleted the duplicate SI and SM performed the Regenerate EOD File but the Consolidated EJ FIle for May 22, 2025 is still missing.
7.Root Cause:
- The reconciliation logic still usesMySQL, since reconciliation is donedaily. However, because ofdata archiving, MySQL only keepsone month of data, so it cannot find the data fromMay last year, which causes the reconciliation to get stuck and theConsolidated EJ is not generated.

Temporary Solution:
- Our R&D Team will manually make the reconciliation successful and then re-run the file in order to have the Consolidated EJ FIle for May 22, 2025.

Long Term Solution:
- We added this in Problem Management for further discussion and to review and sort out the reconciliation business scenarios.

8. Maam Chanda approved and our R&D Team re-run the file and the Consolidated EJ FIlefor May 22, 2025 already exist.
9. Resolved.

【Missing consolidated EJ File of SFTP】
问题: Missing consolidated EJ File of SFTP

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Application Issue

问题描述: Missing consolidated EJ File of SFTP BAGUIO dated May 22, 2025

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:DMall Bug/The reconciliation logic still usesMySQL, since reconciliation is donedaily. However, because ofdata archiving, MySQL only keepsone month of data, so it cannot find the data fromMay last year, which causes the reconciliation to get stuck and theConsolidated EJ is not generated.
Problem # 320
Related to ticket#6370297


Issue Description:Missing consolidated EJ File of SFTP

Troubleshooting process:
1.Acknowledge the ticket.
2.An online order was picked up across different POS machines. During this process when the POS was in the online order page, the POS restarted. After the restart, the recovery mechanism pushed this online order to the cloudeven though payment was not completed, so it should not have been pushed (DMall Bug).
3. This isProblem 170, which was released to production on2025-09-17(version202509_4_PRODFIX_POS).4. However, the order happened inMay, before the fix was applied, so it was not covered.
5. This issue causedone extra receiptto be generated. The original order and receipt data themselves are correct.
6. Our Team already deleted the duplicate SI and SM performed the Regenerate EOD File but the Consolidated EJ FIle for May 22, 2025 is still missing.
7.Root Cause:
- The reconciliation logic still usesMySQL, since reconciliation is donedaily. However, because ofdata archiving, MySQL only keepsone month of data, so it cannot find the data fromMay last year, which causes the reconciliation to get stuck and theConsolidated EJ is not generated.

Temporary Solution:
- Our R&D Team will manually make the reconciliation successful and then re-run the file in order to have the Consolidated EJ FIle for May 22, 2025.

Long Term Solution:
- We added this in Problem Management for further discussion and to review and sort out the reconciliation business scenarios.

8. Maam Chanda approved and our R&D Team re-run the file and the Consolidated EJ FIlefor May 22, 2025 already exist.
9. Resolved.

【UNAUTHORIZED TERM Z POS 37】
问题: UNAUTHORIZED TERM Z POS 37

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

                       &nbs

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause: 


Issue Description:


Troubleshooting process:
1. The reason why the POS already have a Terminal - Z even though it's still not 11:59pm is because, the cashier performs a manual Term - Z.2. If you perform a manual Term - Z, you can still do sign-on, sign out, scan articles, but you are not allowed to have any more transactions, therefore you can only cancel the orders that you scanned.






3. Additionally, there is also a pop up message in the POS that the"POS has completed TermZ and not allowed to process any transaction today, please try again tomorrow"


4. We recommend not doing a manual Term-Z and just let it generate automatically at 11:59 PM.
5. Resolved.

根因分类: Network / Connectivity Failure

具体根因: Network - ISP Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:


Hello,

I would like to raise the issue encountered today after cashier's pre commit. It was noticed that pre commit resulted with high cash shortages and ove

解决摘要: --

解决方案:
Define Issue:POS pre-commit data is not accurate

Root Cause Analysis:POS connection issue / Offline ISP
POS can't connect to the ISP and Cloud during shift handover; uses the POS local data.

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket.
2.Based on the logs and continuous ping, the POScan't connect to the ISP and the Cloud during shift handover therefore the system utilized the POS local data for the pre-commit records.
3. Also based on the monitoring tool, the ISP of SSM Rosaleswas offline during and after the pre-commit.
4. Informed the store that the pre-commit data may not be fully accurate; however, the POS Real-time Sales and Term-Z net amounts remain balanced. Therefore, no discrepancies are expected during the Accounting audit. This behavior is considered normal under such circumstances.
5.Resolved the ticket.

【Unable to start the dmall, response: SI# continuity exception, please contact IT】
问题: Unable to start the dmall, response: SI# continuity exception, please contact IT

根因分类: Application Exit / Close

具体根因: Apps - Application Restart

问题描述: Issue:Unable to start the dmall, Response: SI# continuity exception, please contact IT
Asset Details:
Brand / Model: POS-0073
Serial Number: (2) 202412164
Asset Code: POS-0073 (2) 202412164
AcquisitionDate:

What:U

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:Unable to start the dmall, response: SI# continuity exception, please contact IT
Root Cause Analysis: POS Application Crashed

Resolution:
- Acknowledged the ticket.
- Coordinate with out R&D.
-Upon having conversation with store Customer Service Assistant Maam Joanna, she confirmed that the POS021 experienced application crashed for several times since december 21. They encountered this scenerio when cashier having a transactions andcausing some interruptions in the sales process.at noong december 21, nung nag crashed ang POS Application, dito na nagkaron ng SI# Continuity.There is no timeout error in the Continuous ping and this POS did not encounter a windows update.-According to our R&D Team, these are the impacts of this incident:
-Due to the POS multiple shutdowns, the sequence in the POS local database did not increase which also leads to POSto stuck on the Login Interface with the Error Message"Sl# continuity exception, please contact IT for help".

Solution:
Our R&D Team will also change the sequence in POS Local Database. The sequence record was 14803 which needs to be increased to 14804 so that when the POS used again, the next order SI should be 14804.

Long Term - Solution:The SI exception serves as a built-in safeguard in the POS system to prevent sequence discontinuity of SI numbers. When a discontinuity is detected, the POS is intentionally disabled to ensure data integrity. Our R&D Team will continue to optimize the mechanism for handling SI exceptions to minimize future occurrences.

- Tickets Resolved.

Release Notes/Version:-Remarks/Recommendation:-
Data Collection/References:-

【REQUEST FOR DELETION OF STO】
问题: REQUEST FOR DELETION OF STO

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Application Issue

问题描述: Type: Request
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue:

This is to request for Deletion of the following STO due to no available vehicle to transfer & stocks already depleted in the store

STO: 2035652861
DN: 0074812

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root cause:
Store is requesting for deletion of STO2035652861 with article 20252654 due to noavailable vehicle to transfer & stocks already depleted in the store. But based on checking, STO2035652861 was already processed by SSM Batangas with a received quantity of 0 (meaning not served). Despite this, no STDR was created since the SAP Post status of this transaction remain "Posting" because DMall system currently does not support fully unserved store to store STO.

Solution:
1. DMall tagged the SAP Post status of Reference Order:IB10055202512280001 to "No Need".
2. DMall manually triggered the creation of the STDR.

【SMCO IMALL ANTIPOLO [2861] Integration Inventory 2025 December 29 - Error Msg: Deficit of SL Unrestricted-use 29 PC : 10031783 2861 0003】
问题: SMCO IMALL ANTIPOLO [2861] Integration Inventory 2025 December 29 - Error Msg: Deficit of SL Unrestricted-use 29 PC : 10031783 2861 0003

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Apps - User Action Issue

问题描述: New Ticket Creation Template






Contact Person: *




DMall Support Team






Contact Number / MS Teams: *




09686165958






Email Address: *




dmall2helpdesk@dmall.com






AD ID: *




FRG0023






Affected Markets User:

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause: 
Based on our investigation, RO25CT3055 was immediately rejected upon creation. At the time of the transaction (4:39 PM on December 29, 2025), the available inventory was only 35 pieces because the initial TP-311 movement from SLOC 0001 to SLOC 0003 had not yet been posted and was only posted at 4:40 PM on the same day, resulting in a deficit of 29 pieces.

However, transaction IO12861202512290014 (TP-311 from SLOC 0003 to SLOC 0001) was pushed through in Dmall but was not posted in SAP. Since the transaction was rejected, OPC performed the necessary settlement.

Resolution:
The store submitted a request letter to OPC. OPC posted TP-311 from SLOC 0003 to SLOC 0001 in SAP for the affected article, and Dmall tagged the reference order IO12861202512290014 as “No Need.”

09686165958






Email Address: *




dmall2helpdesk@dmall.com






AD ID: *




FRG0023






Affected Markets User:

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause analysis: R&D identified this as a system bug similar to tickets 6149387 and 6267703, where returned goods created via the PDA show a quantity of 0, causing inventory movement failures. The same issue may occur when creating return orders through the app, with item quantities appearing as 0.


Resolution:

This will be added toProblem List No. 244.
A fix will be implemented to ensure that when submitting returned goods via the PDA, the return quantity cannot be less than or equal to zero.
Our R&D will mark this as“No Need.”​

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Report / Data Extraction

问题描述: Issue: (Briefly describe the
issue/concerns and attach a screenshot or evidence)

Asset Details:
Brand / Model:
Serial Number:
Asset Code:
AcquisitionDate:

What: (Details and expected
result/behavior)

When: (Date and time en

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:HOURLY SALES MONITORING AT DMALL IS NOT UPDATED. NO SALES APPEAR FROM 6:00PM ONWARDSRoot Cause Analysis:Defect from DMall

Resolution:
Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated the issue to our R&D Team.
Based on our investigation, there was alarge data volume reaching the system’s processing capacity threshold, which triggered frequent garbage collection (GC) events and delays in the Hourly Sales Page.
DMall increased the threshold of incoming data to processed the delay sales report and it was generated successfully.
Proceeds in resolving the ticket.

【NO EOD FILES】
问题: NO EOD FILES

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

* SSM ILOILO "0745"- ISP RTO (Connection Down)
-Already escalated to TSG support can now access ISP application
-Perform manual reconciliation but still no

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:User Error - Cashier forget to scan the other article of the customer and did not check the card validity of the customer.

Issue Description:NO EOD FILES

Troubleshooting process:
1. Acknowledge the ticket.
2. Report in our R&D Team.
3. Called the store.
4. After discussing the matter with the store manager, they explained that during the transaction, the cashier failed to scan three items, which led them to void the transaction. The customer used SMAC points worth PHP 200, which were already deducted from the customer’s account but had not yet been reflected in the system. As a result, the manager created a CPR(Cashier Problem Report).

5. For reference, this is the new transaction that they do after the void.

Receipt#:559551007251230143021290037




6. We have included this underProblem Management #293for further discussion on how to handle similar scenarios in the future.


7. We would like also to inform that is it confirmed by SM Application Support that the EOD Files for SSM Iloilo are already completed.

8. Our R&D Team already perform the proposed solution which is passed the void manually.(set to refund success).

问题: STDR SETTLEMENT_UNSERVED STO

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: Ticket Creation Template
Description of your issue or request
STDR SETTLEMENT FOR THE UNSERVED STO(STORE TO STORE) FROM SSM MANDALUYONG TO SSM SUN RESIDENCES. DUE TO WRONG CREATION OF STO RECEIVING SITE.
 STO#2035596563 DN#74678770. 
ARTICLE#2049781

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:
 This issue was caused by the incorrect creation of the STO receiving site. Upon further checking, SSM Sun Residences (receiving site) performed a TP-311 movement from SLOC 0001 to SLOC 0007 for 35 pieces of article 20339460 and 50 pieces of article 20497810 after fully pulling STO 2035596563, with the remark “WRONG STORE CODE USED AS STO. INTENDED FOR JAZZ RESIDENCE.”
Note:
 This is not an unserved transaction, as the store fully received the STO.
Resolution:
 The store submitted a request letter to OPC. OPC performed movement type 989 (Site to Site Transafer) from SLOC 0007 of SSM Sun Residences to SLOC 0001 of SSM Mandaluyong.

dmall2helpdesk@dmall.com

FRG0023






Affected Markets User:

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause: 
Based on our investigation, IO10875202601040008 (TP-311, from SLOC 2 to SLOC 1) was immediately processed after IO10875202601040007 (TP-311, from SLOC 1 to SLOC 2). At the time of the transaction for IO10875202601040008 (4:04 PM on January 4, 2026), the available inventory in SAP was zero (0), resulting in a deficit of 32 pieces.

Issue Description:DMallAppsConcern: No Assigned Sales Invoice Number POS049 TD05/22/2025

【cannot print good receipt】
问题: cannot print good receipt

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Apps - User Inquiry / Knowledge

问题描述: Ticket Creation Template
Description of your issue or request
cannot print good return receipt
Affected Application:
good dispatch
Affected Asset No.

Screenshot of the issue if needed

Contact Person:
madel San Roque
C

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:cannot print good receipt
Root Cause Analysis:Inquiry / User Knowledge

Resolution:
The ticket has been acknowledged.
The store reported that the RPO created on November 22, 2025, could not be found in Goods Dispatch on the DMall web, with a disposal date of December 08, 2025.
Upon verification in DMall, the RPO was visible when searched using the created date. Based on the screenshot provided, the issue occurred because the store was filtering using the disposal date.
The store was advised to filter by the created date, and they confirmed via phone call that the RPO is now visible. We will proceed with closing this ticket.

【NO EOD FILES】
问题: NO EOD FILES

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Application Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:


For 0014 SVI BACOOR (BAC)

- Upon checking by POS Support in DMALL OS , E.O.D. for January 08, 2026 transaction date was successful but NO E.O.D. files were generat

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause:Defect from DMall


Issue Description:NO EOD FILES​


Troubleshooting process:
Investigation:
Our R&D findings show that during order processing, some items within the affected orders were being manually updated by Masterdata at the same time. As a result, when the system queried the item information, the barcode data was missing.
The investigation showed that certain orders from these stores had missing item barcodes in their order details, resulting in failed generation of sales transaction records.
Receipt No. 557481014260108122101200061



Temporary Solution:
Our R&D Team will manually add/restore the missing item barcodes to the order information.

Long-term Solution:
Execute in order and add transaction control to ensure that barcode data is not lost in case of exceptions.And the plan is to release or deploy the long-term solution in the UAT environment on January 15, 2026.

Ticket resolved​

【SSM BALIWAG [0754] IBMS Integration logs 2026 JANUARY 09 - Error Msg: Deficit of SL Unrestricted-use 349 PC : 20251809 0754 0003】
问题: SSM BALIWAG [0754] IBMS Integration logs 2026 JANUARY 09 - Error Msg: Deficit of SL Unrestricted-use 349 PC : 20251809 0754 0003

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Others

问题描述: New Ticket Creation Template






Contact Person: *




DMall Support Team






Contact Number / MS Teams: *




09686165958






Email Address: *




dmall2helpdesk@dmall.com






AD ID: *




FRG0023






Affected Markets User:

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Root Cause: The root cause was an incorrect sequence of data sent to SAP. The RO26192951 was created and withdraw within one minute (January 9, 2026, 19:43). The transfer posting from SLOC 0003 to SLOC 0001 was sent to SAP first, ahead of the transfer posting from SLOC 0001 to SLOC 0003, resulting in a deficit for the affected articles. 
However, the transaction was pushed through in Dmall and was not posted in SAP.

Resolution: As temporary solution, Dmall will manually repost transaction IO10754202601090066 once approved by the IT Heads. This issue has already been added to Problem List 104 for the long-term solution.

Issue: VP Saleset article setting
Resolution: MD corrected the article setting and store proceed with the adjustment

【UNABLE TO POST STDR (STORE TO STORE STO)】
问题: UNABLE TO POST STDR (STORE TO STORE STO)

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Others

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:



Good day,

For your assistance regarding posting of stdr (store to store), Per checking still no GR # in SAP. but upon entering DN in PDA there a msg &

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Issue Summary
The store encountered an error: “A RECEIPT HAS BEEN CREATED FOR THIS DN”, which resulted in the STO being fully unserved and prevented the posting of STDR.
Affected documents: 
STO#: 2035640385
DN#: 74809157
Upon checking DMall, the transaction was already processed and a GR was created.
However, no STDR was generated because the SAP Post status remained as “Posting”, causing the transaction to be stuck.

Action Taken / Immediate Solution
Based on R&D’s recommendation:
DMall will update the SAP Post status of the reference order IB10779202601120008 to “No Need.”
DMall will manually trigger the creation of the STDR to complete the process.

Long-Term Action
The issue has been logged under Problem List 183 for permanent resolution and prevention of recurrence.
